Fireflies produce a \"cold light\", with no infrared or ultraviolet frequencies. A few days after mating, a female lays her fertilized eggs on or just below the surface of the ground. The eggs hatch three to four weeks later, and the larvae feed until the end of the summer. The web color aqua is identical to the web color cyan, also sometimes called electric cyan, one of the three secondary colors of the RGB color model used on computer and television displays. {"ex_id": "test_1328", "sentence": "A walrus never eats oysters near the sea shore.", "label": "false", "entity": "Walrus", "en_wiki_pageid": "33709", "entity_mention_loc": [[2, 8]], "dpr": [{"id": "kilt:14933523", "title": "Walrus", "text": "walrus.
